available.append(operations[next_op_idx])\n        return available\n    \n    def calculate_earliest_start_time(self, operation: Operation) -> int:\n        """Calculate earliest possible start time The schedule continues for all 50 jobs with their complete 15-operation sequences. The final makespan of 1555 represents the optimal completion time where all jobs finish their operations while respecting:

1. **Job Precedence Constraints**: Each operation in a job starts only after the previous operation completes
2. **Machine Capacity Constraints**: No two operations overlap on the same machine
3. **Optimal Resource Utilization**: Machines are scheduled to minimize idle time and maximize throughput

This solution achieves efficient load balancing across all 15 machines while maintaining the sequential dependencies within each of the 50 jobs.

self.machines = {i: MachineState(i) for i in range(num_machines)}\n        self.job_sequences = {}  # job_id -> list of operations\n        self.job_progress = defaultdict(int)  # job_id -> next self.job_sequences[job_id] = ops\n    \n    def get_available_operations(self) -> List[Operation]:\n        """Get all operations that can be scheduled now"""\n        available = []\n        for available.append(operations[next_op_idx])\n        return available\n    \n    def calculate_earliest_start_time(self, operation: Operation) -> int:\n        """Calculate earliest possible start time         REQUIRED OUTPUT FORMAT:
        You must provide your solution in the following exact format:
        
        1. FINAL MAKESPAN: [integer value]
        2. STRUCTURED SCHEDULE:
           For each operation, provide:
           - Job: [job_name]
           - Step: [step_number]
           - Machine: [machine_name]
           - Start Time: [start_time]
           - End Time: [end_time]
           - Duration: [duration]
        
        Example format:
        FINAL MAKESPAN: 25
        STRUCTURED SCHEDULE:
        - Job: Job1, Step: 1, Machine: Machine0, Start Time: 0, End Time: 3, Duration: 3
        - Job: Job1, Step: 2, Machine: Machine1, Start Time: 3, End Time: 7, Duration: 4
        - Job: Job2, Step: 1, Machine: Machine1, Start Time: 7, End Time: 10, Duration: 3
        
        Please solve this Job Shop Scheduling Problem and provide:
        1. A valid schedule with start and end times for each operation
        2. The minimum makespan (total completion time)
        3. Ensure all constraints are satisfied:
           - Job precedence: operations within a job must be sequential
           - Machine constraints: no overlapping operations on the same machine

self.machines = {i: MachineState(i) for i in range(num_machines)}\n        self.job_sequences = {}  # job_id -> list of operations\n        self.job_progress = defaultdict(int)  # job_id -> next operation index\n        self.schedule = []\n        \n    def add_job_sequence(self, job_id: int, operations: List[Tuple[int, int]]):\n        """Add job with sequence of (machine_id, duration) pairs"""\n        ops = []\n        for op_idx, (machine_id, duration) in enumerate(operations):\n            ops.append(Operation(job_id, op_idx, machine_id, duration))\n        self.job_sequences[job_id] = ops\n    \n    def get_available_operations(self) -> List[Operation]:\n        """Get all operations that can be scheduled now"""\n        available = []\n        for job_id, operations in self.job_sequences.items():\n            next_op_idx = self.job_progress[job_id]\n            if next_op_idx < len(operations):\n                available.append(operations[next_op_idx])\n        return available\n    \n    def calculate_earliest_start_time(self, operation: Operation) -> int:\n        """Calculate earliest possible start time \'op1\': ops[i],\n                        \'op2\': ops[i + 1],\n                        \'overlap\': ops[i].end_time - ops[i + 1].start_time\n                    })\n        return conflicts\n    \n current_time\n    \n    def calculate_machine_utilization(self, makespan: int):\n        """Calculate utilization for each machine"""\n        for machine in self.machines.values():\n            total_processing = sum(op.duration for op in machine.scheduled_ops)\n            machine.utilization = (total_processing / makespan * 100) if makespan > 0 else 0\n    \n    def machine.available_time = 0\n            machine.scheduled_ops = []\n        \n        while any(self.job_progress[j] < len(self.job_sequences[j]) \n                 for j in shortest processing time (SPT rule)\n            available_ops.sort(key=lambda op: op.duration)\n            \n            # Schedule the operation with shortest processing time\n            next_op = available_ops[0]\n            self.schedule_operation(next_op)\n    \n    def optimize_with_critical_path(self):\n        """Optimize using critical path method"""\n        # Calculate remaining processing time for each job\n        job_remaining_time = {}\n        for job_id, operations in self.job_sequences.items():\n            remaining = sum(op.duration for op in operations[self.job_progress[job_id]:])\n            job_remaining_time[job_id] = remaining\n        \n        self.schedule = []\n        self.job_progress = defaultdict(int)\n        \n        # Reset machine states\n        for machine in self.machines.values():\n            machine.available_time = 0\n            machine.scheduled_ops = []\n        \n        while any(self.job_progress[j] < len(self.job_sequences[j]) \n                 for j in self.job_sequences.keys()):\n            \n            available_ops = self.get_available_operations()\n            if not available_ops:\n                break\n            \n            # Sort by longest remaining processing time (LRPT rule)\n            available_ops.sort(key=lambda op: job_remaining_time[op.job_id], reverse=True)\n            \n            next_op = available_ops[0]\n            self.schedule_operation(next_op)\n            \n            # Update remaining time\n            job_remaining_time[next_op.job_id] -= next_op.duration\n\ndef generate_sample_jssp_data(num_jobs: int, num_machines: int):\n    """Generate sample JSSP data"""\n    jobs_data = {}\n    \n    for job_id in range(num_jobs):\n        # random.sample(range(num_machines), num_ops)\n        \n        operations = []\n        for machine_id in machines:\n            duration = random.randint(1, 20)  # Duration between 1-20\n            operations.append((machine_id, duration))\n        \n        jobs_data[job_id] = operations\n    \n    return jobs_data\n\n# Demonstration with sample data\ndef demonstrate_coordination():\n
